#include <cmath>
#include <vector>

using namespace std;

double distance(double x1, double y1, double x2, double y2) {
    return sqrt(pow(x1 - x2, 2) + pow(y1 - y2, 2));
}

int main() {
    const int N = 6;
    vector<double> t = {1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6};
    vector<double> y = {2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7};

    double max_distance = 0;
    double x1, y1, x2, y2;

    for (int i = 0; i < N; ++i) {
        for (int j = i + 1; j < N; ++j) {
            double d = distance(t[i], y[i], t[j], y[j]);
            if (d > max_distance) {
                max_distance = d;
                x1 = t[i];
                y1 = y[i];
                x2 = t[j];
                y2 = y[j];
            }
        }
    }

    cout << "Две наиболее удаленные точки: (" << x1 << ", " << y1 << ") и (" << x2 << ", " << y2 << ")" << endl;

    return 0;

section .data
    hello db 'Привет, мир!', 0

section .text
    global _start

_start:
    ; Устанавливаем кодировку Windows-1251
    mov eax, 1200h
    call SetConsoleOutputCP

    ; Выводим "Привет, мир!" на экран
    mov eax, 4
    mov ebx, 1
    mov ecx, hello
    mov edx, 24
    int 80h

    ; Завершаем программу
    mov eax, 1
    xor ebx, ebx
    int 80h

section .bss
    resb 1

section .text
global SetConsoleOutputCP
SetConsoleOutputCP:
    push ebp
    mov ebp, esp
    mov eax, [ebp + 8]
    mov ebx, 0
    push ebx
    push eax
    call [GetStdHandle]
    mov ebx, eax
    push ebx
    push 1
    call [SetConsoleOutputCP]
    pop ebp
    ret

    SetConsoleOutputCP dd 0 - Type: Text  |  ChatID: -1002247934490
